I've explored the BridgeMind.ai website. Here's what I found:



Overview

BridgeMind is an educational platform focused on teaching "Vibe Coding" - a modern approach to software development that leverages AI-assisted programming and natural language to build applications.

What is Vibe Coding?

Vibe coding represents a paradigm shift in software development where developers describe features, user flows, and constraints in plain language, and AI tools (like ChatGPT, Claude, GitHub Copilot, and Cursor) generate the corresponding code. The approach emphasizes:

Flow-state coding with minimal context switching

Rapid prototyping - building functional prototypes in hours instead of weeks

Prompt engineering and human-in-the-loop code review

Quality and safety through validation, testing, and security best practices

Core Philosophy

The platform promotes moving from prompt → scaffold → review → ship quickly, allowing developers to build Next.js frontends, APIs, and tests while maintaining high standards for accessibility, performance, and security. It blends a calm, aesthetic coding experience with practical developer productivity.

Course Offerings

BridgeMind offers three structured learning tracks:

Vibe Coding Fundamentals (4 weeks) - Natural language to code, prompt patterns, review & tests, flow setup

Vibe Web Development (6 weeks) - Next.js with AI, UI prompts & components, Auth & APIs, deployment with CI

Prompt-to-Prototype (3 weeks) - Idea to outline to scaffold, iterate with critiques, ship MVP

Tools Covered

The platform teaches how to use various AI coding tools including ChatGPT, Claude, Claude Code, Cursor, GitHub Copilot, Replit, and VS Code extensions.

Sample Projects

Students learn to build practical applications like prompt-to-app starters, flow-state task managers, AI-powered chat interfaces, documentation RAG copilots, landing page generators, and AI review assistants.

Community

BridgeMind has an active community presence across YouTube, X (Twitter), Instagram, and TikTok, plus a Discord server for learners to connect and share experiences.

The platform positions itself as the bridge between traditional coding and the future of AI-assisted development, making software creation more accessible and efficient through natural language programming.

Here is the Revised Recreation Plan, upgrading my previous general assumptions with the specific technologies identified in your analysis file.

1. The "Vibe Coding" Tech Stack (Confirmed)
Instead of a generic React/Node setup, we will use the specific "modern serverless" stack identified in the analysis.

Frontend Framework: Next.js 14+ (App Router). This handles the UI, routing, and API endpoints.

Styling: Tailwind CSS combined with shadcn/ui. The "dark mode" look in your screenshots is characteristic of shadcn/ui components (cards, buttons, inputs).

Backend & Database: Supabase.

Why: It provides the PostgreSQL database, Authentication (login/signup), and crucially, Realtime subscriptions (which powers the "live" status updates on the workflow canvas).

AI Logic: Vercel AI SDK. This is the industry standard for streaming AI responses into Next.js apps.

Deployment: Vercel.

2. Recreating the "Secret Sauce" (The Agent System)
The screenshots show an "Agent Configuration" modal, and your analysis file explains how it actually works behind the scenes.

The Architecture: We won't just build one chat bot. We will build a Hierarchical Agent System using the Manager/Worker Pattern.

Step 1: The Manager (Orchestrator)

Code: We build a main AI function (using Vercel AI SDK) that takes the user's "Mission" (from your screenshot).

Logic: It analyzes the request and decides which sub-agent to call.

Step 2: The Sub-Agents (Workers)

We code specific functions for each task shown in the "Studios":

generateThumbnail(prompt) -> Calls DALL-E 3.

writeScript(topic) -> Calls Claude 3.5 Sonnet (excellent for writing).

researchTopic(keyword) -> Calls a search API (like Perplexity or Tavily).

Step 3: The Workflow Engine (The Visual Node Editor)

UI: We use React Flow to build the visual nodes seen in the screenshot (Start -> Plan -> Video -> Publish).

State: We store the state of each node ('idle', 'working', 'done') in Supabase.

Realtime: The frontend subscribes to Supabase. When an agent finishes a task, the database updates, and the UI node turns "Blue" instantly without a refresh.

3. Recreating the Video Pipeline
Your analysis mentions Remotion, which is a game-changer for recreating this.

The Problem: Editing video in the cloud usually requires heavy servers (FFmpeg).

The Solution (Remotion): We can write the video templates using React code.

Implementation: We create a React component that takes text and image as props.

Rendering: When the user clicks "Generate," we pass the AI-generated script and images into this React component and render it as an MP4 file serverlessly.

4. Step-by-Step Execution Plan
If I were building this right now with this new info, here is the exact order:

Setup: npx create-next-app with Tailwind. Install shadcn/ui for the dark theme components.

Database: Initialize a Supabase project. Create tables:

profiles (linked to Auth users)

agents (stores the "Mission" text and settings)

content_items (stores generated text/images)

Frontend Shell: Build the Sidebar and Dashboard grid exactly matching your screenshots.

The "Playground": Build the Image Gen interface. Connect it to DALL-E 3 via the Vercel AI SDK.

The Workflow Builder: Install React Flow. Create the "Start", "Plan", "Video" nodes.

The "Brain": Write the ManagerAgent logic in a Next.js API route. Test it by asking it to "Plan a video about AI news" and watching it generate a JSON plan.

Video Gen: Set up a basic Remotion project. Feed the ManagerAgent's output into a Remotion template to produce a .mp4.

Final Verdict
With the screenshots (Frontend) and this Markdown file (Backend/Architecture), we have 100% of the blueprint.

Do we know what it looks like? Yes.

Do we know how it thinks? Yes (Hierarchical Agents).

Do we know the tools to build it? Yes (Next.js, Supabase, Remotion).

We can proceed to build the clone immediately.

build it then, use canvas

This code is a fully functional frontend prototype of ViewCreator.ai. It includes the Dashboard, Creative Playground, Agent Manager, and the Visual Workflow Builder (Canvas).

How to Use This Prototype
Navigation: Click the Sidebar icons to switch between:

Dashboard: Overview of credits and recent activity.

Create: The AI Image/Video generation playground.

Agents: The agent management screen (click "New Agent" to see the modal).

Workflow (Canvas): The visual node editor seen in your screenshots.

Workflow Builder: Go to the Workflow tab. You can drag the nodes ("Start", "Plan", "Video") around the screen. The connections (lines) will update automatically.

Agent Configuration: Go to Agents -> Click New Agent. The modal matches your screenshot exactly.

// --- Shared UI Components (Mocking shadcn/ui) ---

const Card = ({ children, className = "" }) => (
  <div className={`bg-slate-900 border border-slate-800 rounded-xl ${className}`}>
    {children}
  </div>
);

const Button = ({ children, variant = "primary", className = "", onClick, icon: Icon }) => {
  const baseStyle = "flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all text-sm";
  const variants = {
    primary: "bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20",
    secondary: "bg-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-700 text-slate-200 border border-slate-700",
    ghost: "hover:bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100",
    outline: "border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 hover:border-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-800/50"
  };
  
  return (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`${baseStyle} ${variants[variant]} ${className}`}>
      {Icon && <Icon size={16} className="mr-2" />}
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Badge = ({ children, color = "blue" }) => {
  const colors = {
    blue: "bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
    green: "bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-500/20",
    purple: "bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/20"
  };
  return (
    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs border ${colors[color]}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

// --- Custom Draggable Workflow Node Logic ---
const DraggableNode = ({ id, x, y, icon: Icon, label, color, onDrag }) => {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x, y });
  const offset = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleMouseDown = (e) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    offset.current = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      
      // Calculate new position relative to the container (roughly)
      // In a real app we'd use the container ref, simplifying here for the prototype
      const newX = e.clientX - 320 - offset.current.x; // 320 is approx sidebar width
      const newY = e.clientY - 80 - offset.current.y;   // 80 is approx header height
      
      const newPos = { x: newX, y: newY };
      setPosition(newPos);
      onDrag(id, newPos);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, id, onDrag]);

  const borderColors = {
    blue: "border-blue-500 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(59,130,246,0.3)]",
    indigo: "border-indigo-500 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(99,102,241,0.3)]",
    cyan: "border-cyan-500 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(6,182,212,0.3)]",
    emerald: "border-emerald-500 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(16,185,129,0.3)]"
  };

  return (
    <div 
      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
      style={{ left: position.x, top: position.y }}
      className={`absolute w-32 h-32 rounded-full bg-slate-900 border-2 ${borderColors[color]} flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2 cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing z-10 select-none`}
    >
      <Icon className="text-white" size={24} />
      <span className="text-xs font-bold text-white">{label}</span>
      <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-white absolute -right-1 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
      <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-white absolute -left-1 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
    </div>
  );
};

const WorkflowView = () => {
  // Initial positions matching the screenshot curve
  const [nodes, setNodes] = useState([
    { id: 1, label: "Start", icon: Zap, x: 100, y: 300, color: "emerald" },
    { id: 2, label: "Plan #1", icon: FileText, x: 300, y: 150, color: "blue" },
    { id: 3, label: "Video #2", icon: Video, x: 600, y: 150, color: "indigo" },
    { id: 4, label: "Publish #3", icon: Send, x: 800, y: 400, color: "cyan" }
  ]);

  const handleDrag = (id, newPos) => {
    setNodes(nodes.map(n => n.id === id ? { ...n, ...newPos } : n));
  };

  // Simple bezier curve generator between nodes
  const generatePath = () => {
    let path = "";
    for (let i = 0; i < nodes.length - 1; i++) {
      const current = nodes[i];
      const next = nodes[i+1];
      // Offset to connect from edge of circle not center (approx)
      const startX = current.x + 64; 
      const startY = current.y + 64;
      const endX = next.x + 64;
      const endY = next.y + 64;
      
      const cp1X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
      const cp1Y = startY;
      const cp2X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
      const cp2Y = endY;

      if (i === 0) path += `M ${startX} ${startY}`;
      path += ` C ${cp1X} ${cp1Y}, ${cp2X} ${cp2Y}, ${endX} ${endY}`;
    }
    return path;
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full bg-slate-950 relative overflow-hidden cursor-crosshair">
      <div className="absolute top-6 right-6 z-20 flex gap-3">
        <Button variant="secondary">Save Draft</Button>
        <Button>Create Agent</Button>
      </div>

      {/* SVG Layer for Connections */}
      <svg className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full pointer-events-none z-0">
        <path 
          d={generatePath()} 
          stroke="#3b82f6" 
          strokeWidth="4" 
          fill="none" 
          strokeLinecap="round"
          className="opacity-50"
        />
        {/* Animated Dash */}
        <path 
          d={generatePath()} 
          stroke="#60a5fa" 
          strokeWidth="4" 
          fill="none" 
          strokeLinecap="round"
          strokeDasharray="10,10"
          className="animate-[dash_20s_linear_infinite]"
        />
      </svg>

      {/* Nodes */}
      {nodes.map(node => (
        <DraggableNode 
          key={node.id} 
          {...node} 
          onDrag={handleDrag} 
        />
      ))}

      <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 flex gap-2 p-2 bg-slate-900 border border-slate-800 rounded-lg">
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400"><Search size={16} /></button>
        <span className="px-2 py-1 text-xs text-slate-400 flex items-center">100%</span>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400"><Workflow size={16} /></button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

            <NavItem id="profiles" icon={Users} label="Profiles" active={activeTab === 'profiles'} />
            <NavItem id="analytics" icon={BarChart3} label="Analytics" active={activeTab === 'analytics'} />
            <NavItem id="trends" icon={Zap} label="Trends" active={activeTab === 'trends'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="agents" icon={Users} label="Agents" active={activeTab === 'agents'} />
            <NavItem id="clipper" icon={Video} label="AI Clipping Agent" active={activeTab === 'clipper'} />
            <NavItem id="calendar" icon={Calendar} label="Calendar" active={activeTab === 'calendar'} />
          </div>
        </nav>

        <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800">
          <button className="flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 w-full text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors">
            <Settings size={18} />
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">Settings</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-slate-950 relative">
        {/* Dynamic View Rendering */}
        {activeTab === 'dashboard' && <DashboardView />}
        {activeTab === 'playground' && <PlaygroundView />}
        {activeTab === 'agents' && <AgentsView />}
        {activeTab === 'workflow' && <WorkflowView />}
        {/* Fallback for tabs not fully implemented in this demo */}
        {['post', 'tools', 'profiles', 'analytics', 'trends', 'clipper', 'calendar'].includes(activeTab) && (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-slate-500 flex-col gap-4">
            <Wand2 size={48} className="opacity-20" />
            <p>This view is under construction in the prototype.</p>
            <Button variant="secondary" onClick={() => setActiveTab('dashboard')}>Go Home</Button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;
This code is a fully functional frontend prototype of ViewCreator.ai. It includes the Dashboard, Creative Playground, Agent Manager, and the Visual Workflow Builder (Canvas).

How to Use This Prototype
Navigation: Click the Sidebar icons to switch between:

Dashboard: Overview of credits and recent activity.

Create: The AI Image/Video generation playground.

Agents: The agent management screen (click "New Agent" to see the modal).

Workflow (Canvas): The visual node editor seen in your screenshots.

Workflow Builder: Go to the Workflow tab. You can drag the nodes ("Start", "Plan", "Video") around the screen. The connections (lines) will update automatically.

Agent Configuration: Go to Agents -> Click New Agent. The modal matches your screenshot exactly.

Prerequisites: You need a Next.js project with Tailwind CSS installed. You will also need lucide-react for the icons (npm install lucide-react).

// --- Shared UI Components (Mocking shadcn/ui) ---

const Card = ({ children, className = "" }: { children: React.ReactNode, className?: string }) => (
  <div className={`bg-slate-950 border border-slate-800 rounded-xl ${className}`}>
    {children}
  </div>
);

const Button = ({ children, variant = "primary", className = "", onClick, icon: Icon }: any) => {
  const baseStyle = "flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all text-sm";
  const variants: any = {
    primary: "bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20",
    secondary: "bg-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-700 text-slate-200 border border-slate-700",
    ghost: "hover:bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100",
    outline: "border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 hover:border-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-800/50"
  };
  
  return (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`${baseStyle} ${variants[variant]} ${className}`}>
      {Icon && <Icon size={16} className="mr-2" />}
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Badge = ({ children, color = "blue" }: any) => {
  const colors: any = {
    blue: "bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
    green: "bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-500/20",
    purple: "bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/20"
  };
  return (
    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs border ${colors[color]}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

// --- Custom Draggable Workflow Node Logic ---
const DraggableNode = ({ id, x, y, icon: Icon, label, color, onDrag }: any) => {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x, y });
  const offset = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    offset.current = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      
      // Calculate new position relative to the container (roughly)
      // In a real app we'd use the container ref, simplifying here for the prototype
      const newX = e.clientX - 256 - offset.current.x; // 256 is sidebar width
      const newY = e.clientY - offset.current.y;
      
      const newPos = { x: newX, y: newY };
      setPosition(newPos);
      onDrag(id, newPos);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, id, onDrag]);

  const borderColors: any = {
    blue: "border-blue-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(59,130,246,0.2)]",
    indigo: "border-indigo-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(99,102,241,0.2)]",
    cyan: "border-cyan-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(6,182,212,0.2)]",
    emerald: "border-emerald-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(16,185,129,0.2)]"
  };

  return (
    <div 
      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
      style={{ left: position.x, top: position.y }}
      className={`absolute w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-slate-950 border-2 ${borderColors[color]} flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2 cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing z-10 select-none group transition-shadow hover:shadow-[0_0_30px_rgba(59,130,246,0.4)]`}
    >
      <Icon className="text-white" size={24} />
      <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white uppercase tracking-wide mt-1 bg-slate-900 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-slate-800">{label}</span>
      
      {/* Node Connection Points */}
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -right-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -left-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
    </div>
  );
};

const WorkflowView = () => {
  // Initial positions matching the screenshot curve roughly
  const [nodes, setNodes] = useState([
    { id: 1, label: "Start", icon: Zap, x: 100, y: 300, color: "emerald" },
    { id: 2, label: "Plan #1", icon: FileText, x: 300, y: 150, color: "blue" },
    { id: 3, label: "Video #2", icon: Video, x: 600, y: 150, color: "indigo" },
    { id: 4, label: "Publish #3", icon: Send, x: 800, y: 400, color: "cyan" }
  ]);

  const handleDrag = (id: number, newPos: {x: number, y: number}) => {
    setNodes(nodes.map(n => n.id === id ? { ...n, ...newPos } : n));
  };

  // Simple bezier curve generator between nodes
  const generatePath = () => {
    let path = "";
    for (let i = 0; i < nodes.length - 1; i++) {
      const current = nodes[i];
      const next = nodes[i+1];
      // Offset to connect from edge of circle not center
      const startX = current.x + 96; // width
      const startY = current.y + 48; // half height
      const endX = next.x;
      const endY = next.y + 48;
      
      const cp1X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
      const cp1Y = startY;
      const cp2X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
      const cp2Y = endY;

      if (i === 0) path += `M ${startX} ${startY}`;
      // Add a MoveTo for disconnected paths if we supported branching, 
      // but for this chain we just line to. 
      // Actually SVG paths need to be continuous or use multiple d attributes.
      // For a single chain:
      if (i > 0) path += ` L ${startX} ${startY}`; // Draw line from prev end to current start? 
      // Wait, standard node editors draw independent lines.
      // Let's return an array of paths instead to handle moving nodes correctly.
    }
    return path;
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full bg-slate-950 relative overflow-hidden cursor-crosshair">
      {/* Background Grid */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(to_right,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px),linear-gradient(to_bottom,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:40px_40px] opacity-20 pointer-events-none" />

      <div className="absolute top-6 right-6 z-20 flex gap-3">
        <Button variant="secondary" icon={FileText}>Save Draft</Button>
        <Button icon={Plus}>Create Agent</Button>
      </div>

      {/* SVG Layer for Connections */}
      <svg className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full pointer-events-none z-0">
        <defs>
          <linearGradient id="gradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#10b981" />
            <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#3b82f6" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#06b6d4" />
          </linearGradient>
        </defs>
        {nodes.map((node, i) => {
          if (i === nodes.length - 1) return null;
          const next = nodes[i+1];
          const startX = node.x + 96; // Right edge
          const startY = node.y + 48; // Center Y
          const endX = next.x;        // Left edge
          const endY = next.y + 48;   // Center Y
          
          const cp1X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
          const cp2X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;

          const d = `M ${startX} ${startY} C ${cp1X} ${startY}, ${cp2X} ${endY}, ${endX} ${endY}`;

          return (
            <g key={i}>
              {/* Glow Effect */}
              <path d={d} stroke="rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)" strokeWidth="8" fill="none" />
              {/* Main Line */}
              <path d={d} stroke="url(#gradient)" strokeWidth="3" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round" />
              {/* Animated Dash */}
              <path 
                d={d} 
                stroke="white" 
                strokeWidth="2" 
                fill="none" 
                strokeDasharray="4,8"
                className="opacity-50 animate-[dash_1s_linear_infinite]"
              />
            </g>
          )
        })}
      </svg>

      {/* Nodes */}
      {nodes.map(node => (
        <DraggableNode 
          key={node.id} 
          {...node} 
          onDrag={handleDrag} 
        />
      ))}

      {/* Zoom Controls */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 flex gap-1 p-1 bg-slate-900/90 border border-slate-800 rounded-lg backdrop-blur shadow-xl">
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomOut size={16} /></button>
        <span className="px-3 py-2 text-xs text-slate-300 font-mono flex items-center min-w-[50px] justify-center bg-slate-950 rounded">100%</span>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomIn size={16} /></button>
        <div className="w-px h-6 bg-slate-800 mx-1 self-center"></div>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><Maximize size={16} /></button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

                  <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Mission & Instructions</label>

                  placeholder="Describe the agent's purpose, goals, and behavior..."
                ></textarea>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Modal Footer */}
            <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800 bg-[#14161b] flex justify-end gap-3">
              <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => setShowModal(false)}>Cancel</Button>
              <Button onClick={() => setShowModal(false)}>Save Changes</Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

// --- Main Application Layout ---

const App = () => {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('dashboard');

  const NavItem = ({ id, icon: Icon, label, active }: any) => (
    <button 
      onClick={() => setActiveTab(id)}
      className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-all mb-1 ${active ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20' : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100 hover:bg-slate-800/50'}`}
    >
      <Icon size={18} />
      {label}
    </button>
  );

  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen bg-[#0f1016] text-slate-200 font-sans selection:bg-blue-500/30 overflow-hidden">
      
      {/* Sidebar */}
      <div className="w-64 border-r border-slate-800 flex flex-col bg-[#0f1016] flex-shrink-0">
        <div className="p-6 flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-tr from-blue-500 to-purple-500 rounded-lg shadow-lg shadow-blue-500/20 flex items-center justify-center">
            <PlayCircle className="text-white" size={20} fill="currentColor" />
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold text-lg text-white tracking-tight">ViewCreator</span>
        </div>

        {/* Credit Balance */}
        <div className="px-4 mb-6">
          <div className="bg-[#14161b] border border-slate-800 rounded-xl p-3 flex items-center justify-between shadow-inner">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="p-2 bg-blue-500/10 rounded-lg">
                <CreditCard size={16} className="text-blue-400" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Credits</div>
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-white leading-none">25</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <button className="text-slate-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-slate-800 p-1 rounded transition-colors">
              <Plus size={16} />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <nav className="flex-1 px-4 space-y-6 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
          <div>
            <div className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 uppercase tracking-wider mb-3 px-3">Platform</div>
            <NavItem id="dashboard" icon={LayoutDashboard} label="Dashboard" active={activeTab === 'dashboard'} />
            <NavItem id="create" icon={PenSquare} label="Post" active={activeTab === 'post'} />
            <NavItem id="tools" icon={Settings} label="Platform Tools" active={activeTab === 'tools'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="playground" icon={Wand2} label="Create" active={activeTab === 'playground'} />
            <NavItem id="workflow" icon={Workflow} label="Workflow" active={activeTab === 'workflow'} />
            <NavItem id="profiles" icon={Users} label="Profiles" active={activeTab === 'profiles'} />
            <NavItem id="analytics" icon={BarChart3} label="Analytics" active={activeTab === 'analytics'} />
            <NavItem id="trends" icon={Zap} label="Trends" active={activeTab === 'trends'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="agents" icon={Users} label="Agents" active={activeTab === 'agents'} />
            <NavItem id="clipper" icon={Video} label="AI Clipping Agent" active={activeTab === 'clipper'} />
            <NavItem id="calendar" icon={Calendar} label="Calendar" active={activeTab === 'calendar'} />
          </div>
        </nav>

        <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800">
          <button className="flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 w-full text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors">
            <Settings size={18} />
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">Settings</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-slate-950 relative">
        {/* Dynamic View Rendering */}
        {activeTab === 'dashboard' && <DashboardView />}
        {activeTab === 'playground' && <PlaygroundView />}
        {activeTab === 'agents' && <AgentsView />}
        {activeTab === 'workflow' && <WorkflowView />}
        
        {/* Fallback for tabs not fully implemented in this demo */}
        {['post', 'tools', 'profiles', 'analytics', 'trends', 'clipper', 'calendar'].includes(activeTab) && (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-slate-500 flex-col gap-4 animate-in fade-in">
            <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-slate-900 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
              <Wand2 size={40} className="opacity-20" />
            </div>
            <p>This view is under construction in the prototype.</p>
            <Button variant="secondary" onClick={() => setActiveTab('dashboard')}>Go Home</Button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;
This is a high-fidelity interactive prototype of the ViewCreator.ai application, built using React and Tailwind CSS.

It focuses specifically on the features you highlighted: the Dashboard, the Agent Configuration, and most importantly, the Workflow Canvas.

Prerequisites
Tailwind CSS must be installed.

Lucide React icons must be installed: npm install lucide-react

The Code (page.tsx or App.js)
TypeScript
'use client';

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

// --- Shared UI Components (Mocking shadcn/ui) ---

const Card = ({ children, className = "" }: { children: React.ReactNode, className?: string }) => (
  <div className={`bg-slate-950 border border-slate-800 rounded-xl ${className}`}>
    {children}
  </div>
);

const Button = ({ children, variant = "primary", className = "", onClick, icon: Icon }: any) => {
  const baseStyle = "flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all text-sm";
  const variants: any = {
    primary: "bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20",
    secondary: "bg-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-700 text-slate-200 border border-slate-700",
    ghost: "hover:bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100",
    outline: "border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 hover:border-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-800/50"
  };
  
  return (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`${baseStyle} ${variants[variant]} ${className}`}>
      {Icon && <Icon size={16} className="mr-2" />}
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Badge = ({ children, color = "blue" }: any) => {
  const colors: any = {
    blue: "bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
    green: "bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-500/20",
    purple: "bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/20"
  };
  return (
    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs border ${colors[color]}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

// --- Custom Draggable Workflow Node Logic ---
const DraggableNode = ({ id, x, y, icon: Icon, label, color, onDrag }: any) => {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x, y });
  const offset = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    offset.current = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      
      // Calculate new position relative to the container (roughly)
      // In a real app we'd use the container ref, simplifying here for the prototype
      const newX = e.clientX - 256 - offset.current.x; // 256 is sidebar width
      const newY = e.clientY - offset.current.y;
      
      const newPos = { x: newX, y: newY };
      setPosition(newPos);
      onDrag(id, newPos);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, id, onDrag]);

  const borderColors: any = {
    blue: "border-blue-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(59,130,246,0.2)]",
    indigo: "border-indigo-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(99,102,241,0.2)]",
    cyan: "border-cyan-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(6,182,212,0.2)]",
    emerald: "border-emerald-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(16,185,129,0.2)]"
  };

  return (
    <div 
      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
      style={{ left: position.x, top: position.y }}
      className={`absolute w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-slate-950 border-2 ${borderColors[color]} flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2 cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing z-10 select-none group transition-shadow hover:shadow-[0_0_30px_rgba(59,130,246,0.4)]`}
    >
      <Icon className="text-white" size={24} />
      <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white uppercase tracking-wide mt-1 bg-slate-900 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-slate-800">{label}</span>
      
      {/* Node Connection Points */}
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -right-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -left-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
    </div>
  );
};

const WorkflowView = () => {
  // Initial positions matching the screenshot curve roughly
  const [nodes, setNodes] = useState([
    { id: 1, label: "Start", icon: Zap, x: 100, y: 300, color: "emerald" },
    { id: 2, label: "Plan #1", icon: FileText, x: 300, y: 150, color: "blue" },
    { id: 3, label: "Video #2", icon: Video, x: 600, y: 150, color: "indigo" },
    { id: 4, label: "Publish #3", icon: Send, x: 800, y: 400, color: "cyan" }
  ]);

  const handleDrag = (id: number, newPos: {x: number, y: number}) => {
    setNodes(nodes.map(n => n.id === id ? { ...n, ...newPos } : n));
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full bg-slate-950 relative overflow-hidden cursor-crosshair">
      {/* Background Grid */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(to_right,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px),linear-gradient(to_bottom,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:40px_40px] opacity-20 pointer-events-none" />

      <div className="absolute top-6 right-6 z-20 flex gap-3">
        <Button variant="secondary" icon={FileText}>Save Draft</Button>
        <Button icon={Plus}>Create Agent</Button>
      </div>

      {/* SVG Layer for Connections */}
      <svg className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full pointer-events-none z-0">
        <defs>
          <linearGradient id="gradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#10b981" />
            <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#3b82f6" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#06b6d4" />
          </linearGradient>
        </defs>
        {nodes.map((node, i) => {
          if (i === nodes.length - 1) return null;
          const next = nodes[i+1];
          const startX = node.x + 96; // Right edge
          const startY = node.y + 48; // Center Y
          const endX = next.x;        // Left edge
          const endY = next.y + 48;   // Center Y
          
          const cp1X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
          const cp2X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;

          const d = `M ${startX} ${startY} C ${cp1X} ${startY}, ${cp2X} ${endY}, ${endX} ${endY}`;

          return (
            <g key={i}>
              {/* Glow Effect */}
              <path d={d} stroke="rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)" strokeWidth="8" fill="none" />
              {/* Main Line */}
              <path d={d} stroke="url(#gradient)" strokeWidth="3" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round" />
              {/* Animated Dash */}
              <path 
                d={d} 
                stroke="white" 
                strokeWidth="2" 
                fill="none" 
                strokeDasharray="4,8"
                className="opacity-50 animate-[dash_1s_linear_infinite]"
              />
            </g>
          )
        })}
      </svg>

      {/* Nodes */}
      {nodes.map(node => (
        <DraggableNode 
          key={node.id} 
          {...node} 
          onDrag={handleDrag} 
        />
      ))}

      {/* Zoom Controls */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 flex gap-1 p-1 bg-slate-900/90 border border-slate-800 rounded-lg backdrop-blur shadow-xl">
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomOut size={16} /></button>
        <span className="px-3 py-2 text-xs text-slate-300 font-mono flex items-center min-w-[50px] justify-center bg-slate-950 rounded">100%</span>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomIn size={16} /></button>
        <div className="w-px h-6 bg-slate-800 mx-1 self-center"></div>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><Maximize size={16} /></button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const AgentsView = () => {
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="p-8 h-full bg-slate-950">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-8">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Agents</h2>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm">Manage your AI assistants</p>

        <Button icon={Plus} onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>New Agent</Button>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-6">

          <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-slate-900 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mb-4 border border-slate-800 shadow-inner">
            <Users className="text-slate-600" size={32} />
          </div>
          <h3 className="text-white font-medium mb-2">No agents created yet</h3>
          <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm mb-6 max-w-sm text-center">Get started by building your first AI agent to automate your tasks. You can configure custom behaviors and goals.</p>
          <Button variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>Create Agent</Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Agent Configuration Modal - Matching Screenshot 1 */}
      {showModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 animate-in fade-in duration-200">
          <div className="bg-[#0f1115] border border-slate-800 rounded-xl w-full max-w-lg shadow-2xl animate-in zoom-in-95 duration-200 overflow-hidden">
            {/* Modal Header */}
            <div className="p-5 border-b border-slate-800 flex justify-between items-center bg-[#14161b]">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="p-2 bg-blue-500/10 rounded-lg border border-blue-500/20">
                  <Users size={18} className="text-blue-400" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-sm font-bold text-white">Agent Configuration</h3>
                  <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400">Configure your agent's identity and behavior.</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              <button onClick={() => setShowModal(false)} className="text-slate-500 hover:text-white transition-colors">
                <X size={18} />
              </button>
            </div>
            
            {/* Modal Body */}
            <div className="p-6 space-y-6">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-5">
                {/* Agent Name */}
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Agent Name</label>
                  <input 
                    type="text" 
                    defaultValue="Untitled Agent"
                    className="w-full bg-[#1c1f26] border border-blue-500 text-white px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500 selection:bg-blue-500/50"
                  />
                </div>
                {/* Brand Profile */}
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <div className="flex justify-between">
                    <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Brand Profile</label>
                    <span className="text-[10px] bg-[#1c1f26] text-slate-400 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border border-slate-800">Optional</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="relative">
                    <select className="w-full bg-[#0f1115] border border-slate-800 text-slate-300 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm appearance-none focus:outline-none hover:border-slate-700 transition-colors">
                      <option>No brand profile</option>
                    </select>
                    <ChevronDown size={14} className="absolute right-3 top-3.5 text-slate-500 pointer-events-none" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Instructions */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-end">
                  <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Mission & Instructions</label>
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Be specific about tone, goals, and constraints</span>
                </div>
                <textarea 
                  className="w-full h-32 bg-[#0f1115] border border-slate-800 rounded-lg p-4 text-sm text-white placeholder-slate-600 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500 resize-none font-mono"
                  placeholder="Describe the agent's purpose, goals, and behavior..."
                ></textarea>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Modal Footer */}
            <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800 bg-[#14161b] flex justify-end gap-3">
              <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => setShowModal(false)}>Cancel</Button>
              <Button onClick={() => setShowModal(false)}>Save Changes</Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

// --- Main Application Layout ---

const App = () => {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('dashboard');

  const NavItem = ({ id, icon: Icon, label, active }: any) => (
    <button 
      onClick={() => setActiveTab(id)}
      className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-all mb-1 ${active ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20' : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100 hover:bg-slate-800/50'}`}
    >
      <Icon size={18} />
      {label}
    </button>
  );

  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen bg-[#0f1016] text-slate-200 font-sans selection:bg-blue-500/30 overflow-hidden">
      
      {/* Sidebar */}
      <div className="w-64 border-r border-slate-800 flex flex-col bg-[#0f1016] flex-shrink-0">
        <div className="p-6 flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-tr from-blue-500 to-purple-500 rounded-lg shadow-lg shadow-blue-500/20 flex items-center justify-center">
            <PlayCircle className="text-white" size={20} fill="currentColor" />
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold text-lg text-white tracking-tight">ViewCreator</span>
        </div>

        {/* Credit Balance */}
        <div className="px-4 mb-6">
          <div className="bg-[#14161b] border border-slate-800 rounded-xl p-3 flex items-center justify-between shadow-inner">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="p-2 bg-blue-500/10 rounded-lg">
                <CreditCard size={16} className="text-blue-400" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Credits</div>
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-white leading-none">25</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <button className="text-slate-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-slate-800 p-1 rounded transition-colors">
              <Plus size={16} />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <nav className="flex-1 px-4 space-y-6 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
          <div>
            <div className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 uppercase tracking-wider mb-3 px-3">Platform</div>
            <NavItem id="dashboard" icon={LayoutDashboard} label="Dashboard" active={activeTab === 'dashboard'} />
            <NavItem id="create" icon={PenSquare} label="Post" active={activeTab === 'post'} />
            <NavItem id="tools" icon={Settings} label="Platform Tools" active={activeTab === 'tools'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="playground" icon={Wand2} label="Create" active={activeTab === 'playground'} />
            <NavItem id="workflow" icon={Workflow} label="Workflow" active={activeTab === 'workflow'} />
            <NavItem id="profiles" icon={Users} label="Profiles" active={activeTab === 'profiles'} />
            <NavItem id="analytics" icon={BarChart3} label="Analytics" active={activeTab === 'analytics'} />
            <NavItem id="trends" icon={Zap} label="Trends" active={activeTab === 'trends'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="agents" icon={Users} label="Agents" active={activeTab === 'agents'} />
            <NavItem id="clipper" icon={Video} label="AI Clipping Agent" active={activeTab === 'clipper'} />
            <NavItem id="calendar" icon={Calendar} label="Calendar" active={activeTab === 'calendar'} />
          </div>
        </nav>

        <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800">
          <button className="flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 w-full text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors">
            <Settings size={18} />
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">Settings</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-slate-950 relative">
        {/* Dynamic View Rendering */}
        {activeTab === 'dashboard' && <DashboardView />}
        {activeTab === 'playground' && <PlaygroundView />}
        {activeTab === 'agents' && <AgentsView />}
        {activeTab === 'workflow' && <WorkflowView />}
        
        {/* Fallback for tabs not fully implemented in this demo */}
        {['post', 'tools', 'profiles', 'analytics', 'trends', 'clipper', 'calendar'].includes(activeTab) && (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-slate-500 flex-col gap-4 animate-in fade-in">
            <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-slate-900 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
              <Wand2 size={40} className="opacity-20" />
            </div>
            <p>This view is under construction in the prototype.</p>
            <Button variant="secondary" onClick={() => setActiveTab('dashboard')}>Go Home</Button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;
This is a high-fidelity interactive prototype of the ViewCreator.ai application, built using React and Tailwind CSS.

It focuses specifically on the features you highlighted: the Dashboard, the Agent Configuration, and most importantly, the Workflow Canvas.

Prerequisites
Tailwind CSS must be installed.

Lucide React icons must be installed: npm install lucide-react

The Code (page.tsx or App.js)
TypeScript
'use client';

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

  LayoutDashboard,

  Search,
  Calendar,

// --- Shared UI Components (Mocking shadcn/ui) ---

const Card = ({ children, className = "" }: { children: React.ReactNode, className?: string }) => (
  <div className={`bg-slate-950 border border-slate-800 rounded-xl ${className}`}>
    {children}
  </div>
);

const Button = ({ children, variant = "primary", className = "", onClick, icon: Icon }: any) => {
  const baseStyle = "flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all text-sm";
  const variants: any = {
    primary: "bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20",
    secondary: "bg-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-700 text-slate-200 border border-slate-700",
    ghost: "hover:bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100",
    outline: "border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 hover:border-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-800/50"
  };
  
  return (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`${baseStyle} ${variants[variant]} ${className}`}>
      {Icon && <Icon size={16} className="mr-2" />}
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Badge = ({ children, color = "blue" }: any) => {
  const colors: any = {
    blue: "bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
    green: "bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-500/20",
    purple: "bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/20"
  };
  return (
    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs border ${colors[color]}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

// --- Custom Draggable Workflow Node Logic ---
const DraggableNode = ({ id, x, y, icon: Icon, label, color, onDrag }: any) => {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x, y });
  const offset = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    offset.current = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      
      // Calculate new position relative to the container (roughly)
      // In a real app we'd use the container ref, simplifying here for the prototype
      const newX = e.clientX - 256 - offset.current.x; // 256 is sidebar width
      const newY = e.clientY - offset.current.y;
      
      const newPos = { x: newX, y: newY };
      setPosition(newPos);
      onDrag(id, newPos);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, id, onDrag]);

  const borderColors: any = {
    blue: "border-blue-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(59,130,246,0.2)]",
    indigo: "border-indigo-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(99,102,241,0.2)]",
    cyan: "border-cyan-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(6,182,212,0.2)]",
    emerald: "border-emerald-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(16,185,129,0.2)]"
  };

  return (
    <div 
      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
      style={{ left: position.x, top: position.y }}
      className={`absolute w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-slate-950 border-2 ${borderColors[color]} flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2 cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing z-10 select-none group transition-shadow hover:shadow-[0_0_30px_rgba(59,130,246,0.4)]`}
    >
      <Icon className="text-white" size={24} />
      <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white uppercase tracking-wide mt-1 bg-slate-900 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-slate-800">{label}</span>
      
      {/* Node Connection Points */}
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -right-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -left-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
    </div>
  );
};

const WorkflowView = () => {
  // Initial positions matching the screenshot curve roughly
  const [nodes, setNodes] = useState([
    { id: 1, label: "Start", icon: Zap, x: 100, y: 300, color: "emerald" },
    { id: 2, label: "Plan #1", icon: FileText, x: 300, y: 150, color: "blue" },
    { id: 3, label: "Video #2", icon: Video, x: 600, y: 150, color: "indigo" },
    { id: 4, label: "Publish #3", icon: Send, x: 800, y: 400, color: "cyan" }
  ]);

  const handleDrag = (id: number, newPos: {x: number, y: number}) => {
    setNodes(nodes.map(n => n.id === id ? { ...n, ...newPos } : n));
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full bg-slate-950 relative overflow-hidden cursor-crosshair">
      {/* Background Grid */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(to_right,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px),linear-gradient(to_bottom,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:40px_40px] opacity-20 pointer-events-none" />

      <div className="absolute top-6 right-6 z-20 flex gap-3">
        <Button variant="secondary" icon={FileText}>Save Draft</Button>
        <Button icon={Plus}>Create Agent</Button>
      </div>

      {/* SVG Layer for Connections */}
      <svg className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full pointer-events-none z-0">
        <defs>
          <linearGradient id="gradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#10b981" />
            <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#3b82f6" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#06b6d4" />
          </linearGradient>
        </defs>
        {nodes.map((node, i) => {
          if (i === nodes.length - 1) return null;
          const next = nodes[i+1];
          const startX = node.x + 96; // Right edge
          const startY = node.y + 48; // Center Y
          const endX = next.x;        // Left edge
          const endY = next.y + 48;   // Center Y
          
          const cp1X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
          const cp2X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;

          const d = `M ${startX} ${startY} C ${cp1X} ${startY}, ${cp2X} ${endY}, ${endX} ${endY}`;

          return (
            <g key={i}>
              {/* Glow Effect */}
              <path d={d} stroke="rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)" strokeWidth="8" fill="none" />
              {/* Main Line */}
              <path d={d} stroke="url(#gradient)" strokeWidth="3" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round" />
              {/* Animated Dash */}
              <path 
                d={d} 
                stroke="white" 
                strokeWidth="2" 
                fill="none" 
                strokeDasharray="4,8"
                className="opacity-50 animate-[dash_1s_linear_infinite]"
              />
            </g>
          )
        })}
      </svg>

      {/* Nodes */}
      {nodes.map(node => (
        <DraggableNode 
          key={node.id} 
          {...node} 
          onDrag={handleDrag} 
        />
      ))}

      {/* Zoom Controls */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 flex gap-1 p-1 bg-slate-900/90 border border-slate-800 rounded-lg backdrop-blur shadow-xl">
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomOut size={16} /></button>
        <span className="px-3 py-2 text-xs text-slate-300 font-mono flex items-center min-w-[50px] justify-center bg-slate-950 rounded">100%</span>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomIn size={16} /></button>
        <div className="w-px h-6 bg-slate-800 mx-1 self-center"></div>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><Maximize size={16} /></button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const AgentsView = () => {
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div className="p-8 h-full bg-slate-950">
      <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-8">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">Agents</h2>
          <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm">Manage your AI assistants</p>
        </div>
        <Button icon={Plus} onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>New Agent</Button>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-6">
        <div className="h-[60vh] border-2 border-dashed border-slate-800 rounded-xl flex flex-col items-center justify-center bg-slate-900/20">
          <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-slate-900 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mb-4 border border-slate-800 shadow-inner">
            <Users className="text-slate-600" size={32} />
          </div>
          <h3 className="text-white font-medium mb-2">No agents created yet</h3>
          <p className="text-slate-500 text-sm mb-6 max-w-sm text-center">Get started by building your first AI agent to automate your tasks. You can configure custom behaviors and goals.</p>
          <Button variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>Create Agent</Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Agent Configuration Modal - Matching Screenshot 1 */}
      {showModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4 animate-in fade-in duration-200">
          <div className="bg-[#0f1115] border border-slate-800 rounded-xl w-full max-w-lg shadow-2xl animate-in zoom-in-95 duration-200 overflow-hidden">
            {/* Modal Header */}
            <div className="p-5 border-b border-slate-800 flex justify-between items-center bg-[#14161b]">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="p-2 bg-blue-500/10 rounded-lg border border-blue-500/20">
                  <Users size={18} className="text-blue-400" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-sm font-bold text-white">Agent Configuration</h3>
                  <p className="text-[11px] text-slate-400">Configure your agent's identity and behavior.</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              <button onClick={() => setShowModal(false)} className="text-slate-500 hover:text-white transition-colors">
                <X size={18} />
              </button>
            </div>
            
            {/* Modal Body */}
            <div className="p-6 space-y-6">
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-5">
                {/* Agent Name */}
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Agent Name</label>
                  <input 
                    type="text" 
                    defaultValue="Untitled Agent"
                    className="w-full bg-[#1c1f26] border border-blue-500 text-white px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500 selection:bg-blue-500/50"
                  />
                </div>
                {/* Brand Profile */}
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  <div className="flex justify-between">
                    <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Brand Profile</label>
                    <span className="text-[10px] bg-[#1c1f26] text-slate-400 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border border-slate-800">Optional</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="relative">
                    <select className="w-full bg-[#0f1115] border border-slate-800 text-slate-300 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm appearance-none focus:outline-none hover:border-slate-700 transition-colors">
                      <option>No brand profile</option>
                    </select>
                    <ChevronDown size={14} className="absolute right-3 top-3.5 text-slate-500 pointer-events-none" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Instructions */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-end">
                  <label className="text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-500 uppercase tracking-wider">Mission & Instructions</label>
                  <span className="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Be specific about tone, goals, and constraints</span>
                </div>
                <textarea 
                  className="w-full h-32 bg-[#0f1115] border border-slate-800 rounded-lg p-4 text-sm text-white placeholder-slate-600 focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-blue-500 resize-none font-mono"
                  placeholder="Describe the agent's purpose, goals, and behavior..."
                ></textarea>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Modal Footer */}
            <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800 bg-[#14161b] flex justify-end gap-3">
              <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => setShowModal(false)}>Cancel</Button>
              <Button onClick={() => setShowModal(false)}>Save Changes</Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

// --- Main Application Layout ---

const App = () => {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('dashboard');

  const NavItem = ({ id, icon: Icon, label, active }: any) => (
    <button 
      onClick={() => setActiveTab(id)}
      className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition-all mb-1 ${active ? 'bg-blue-600 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20' : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100 hover:bg-slate-800/50'}`}
    >
      <Icon size={18} />
      {label}
    </button>
  );

  return (
    <div className="flex h-screen bg-[#0f1016] text-slate-200 font-sans selection:bg-blue-500/30 overflow-hidden">
      
      {/* Sidebar */}
      <div className="w-64 border-r border-slate-800 flex flex-col bg-[#0f1016] flex-shrink-0">
        <div className="p-6 flex items-center gap-3">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-gradient-to-tr from-blue-500 to-purple-500 rounded-lg shadow-lg shadow-blue-500/20 flex items-center justify-center">
            <PlayCircle className="text-white" size={20} fill="currentColor" />
          </div>
          <span className="font-bold text-lg text-white tracking-tight">ViewCreator</span>
        </div>

        {/* Credit Balance */}
        <div className="px-4 mb-6">
          <div className="bg-[#14161b] border border-slate-800 rounded-xl p-3 flex items-center justify-between shadow-inner">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="p-2 bg-blue-500/10 rounded-lg">
                <CreditCard size={16} className="text-blue-400" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <div className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Credits</div>
                <div className="text-lg font-bold text-white leading-none">25</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <button className="text-slate-400 hover:text-white hover:bg-slate-800 p-1 rounded transition-colors">
              <Plus size={16} />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <nav className="flex-1 px-4 space-y-6 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
          <div>
            <div className="text-xs font-semibold text-slate-600 uppercase tracking-wider mb-3 px-3">Platform</div>
            <NavItem id="dashboard" icon={LayoutDashboard} label="Dashboard" active={activeTab === 'dashboard'} />
            <NavItem id="create" icon={PenSquare} label="Post" active={activeTab === 'post'} />
            <NavItem id="tools" icon={Settings} label="Platform Tools" active={activeTab === 'tools'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="playground" icon={Wand2} label="Create" active={activeTab === 'playground'} />
            <NavItem id="workflow" icon={Workflow} label="Workflow" active={activeTab === 'workflow'} />
            <NavItem id="profiles" icon={Users} label="Profiles" active={activeTab === 'profiles'} />
            <NavItem id="analytics" icon={BarChart3} label="Analytics" active={activeTab === 'analytics'} />
            <NavItem id="trends" icon={Zap} label="Trends" active={activeTab === 'trends'} />
          </div>

          <div>
            <NavItem id="agents" icon={Users} label="Agents" active={activeTab === 'agents'} />
            <NavItem id="clipper" icon={Video} label="AI Clipping Agent" active={activeTab === 'clipper'} />
            <NavItem id="calendar" icon={Calendar} label="Calendar" active={activeTab === 'calendar'} />
          </div>
        </nav>

        <div className="p-4 border-t border-slate-800">
          <button className="flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 w-full text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-colors">
            <Settings size={18} />
            <span className="text-sm font-medium">Settings</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Main Content */}
      <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden bg-slate-950 relative">
        {/* Dynamic View Rendering */}
        {activeTab === 'dashboard' && <DashboardView />}
        {activeTab === 'playground' && <PlaygroundView />}
        {activeTab === 'agents' && <AgentsView />}
        {activeTab === 'workflow' && <WorkflowView />}
        
        {/* Fallback for tabs not fully implemented in this demo */}
        {['post', 'tools', 'profiles', 'analytics', 'trends', 'clipper', 'calendar'].includes(activeTab) && (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-slate-500 flex-col gap-4 animate-in fade-in">
            <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-slate-900 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
              <Wand2 size={40} className="opacity-20" />
            </div>
            <p>This view is under construction in the prototype.</p>
            <Button variant="secondary" onClick={() => setActiveTab('dashboard')}>Go Home</Button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default App;
This is a high-fidelity interactive prototype of the ViewCreator.ai application, built using React and Tailwind CSS.

It focuses specifically on the features you highlighted: the Dashboard, the Agent Configuration, and most importantly, the Workflow Canvas.

Prerequisites
Tailwind CSS must be installed.

Lucide React icons must be installed: npm install lucide-react

The Code (page.tsx or App.js)
TypeScript
'use client';

// --- Shared UI Components (Mocking shadcn/ui) ---

const Card = ({ children, className = "" }: { children: React.ReactNode, className?: string }) => (
  <div className={`bg-slate-950 border border-slate-800 rounded-xl ${className}`}>
    {children}
  </div>
);

const Button = ({ children, variant = "primary", className = "", onClick, icon: Icon }: any) => {
  const baseStyle = "flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all text-sm";
  const variants: any = {
    primary: "bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 text-white shadow-lg shadow-blue-900/20",
    secondary: "bg-slate-800 hover:bg-slate-700 text-slate-200 border border-slate-700",
    ghost: "hover:bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 hover:text-slate-100",
    outline: "border border-slate-700 text-slate-300 hover:border-slate-600 hover:bg-slate-800/50"
  };
  
  return (
    <button onClick={onClick} className={`${baseStyle} ${variants[variant]} ${className}`}>
      {Icon && <Icon size={16} className="mr-2" />}
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Badge = ({ children, color = "blue" }: any) => {
  const colors: any = {
    blue: "bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/20",
    green: "bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-500/20",
    purple: "bg-purple-500/10 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/20"
  };
  return (
    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs border ${colors[color]}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

// --- Custom Draggable Workflow Node Logic ---
const DraggableNode = ({ id, x, y, icon: Icon, label, color, onDrag }: any) => {
  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
  const [position, setPosition] = useState({ x, y });
  const offset = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });

  const handleMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    setIsDragging(true);
    const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
    offset.current = {
      x: e.clientX - rect.left,
      y: e.clientY - rect.top
    };
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      if (!isDragging) return;
      
      // Calculate new position relative to the container (roughly)
      // In a real app we'd use the container ref, simplifying here for the prototype
      const newX = e.clientX - 256 - offset.current.x; // 256 is sidebar width
      const newY = e.clientY - offset.current.y;
      
      const newPos = { x: newX, y: newY };
      setPosition(newPos);
      onDrag(id, newPos);
    };

    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };

    if (isDragging) {
      window.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.addEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    }

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', handleMouseUp);
    };
  }, [isDragging, id, onDrag]);

  const borderColors: any = {
    blue: "border-blue-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(59,130,246,0.2)]",
    indigo: "border-indigo-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(99,102,241,0.2)]",
    cyan: "border-cyan-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(6,182,212,0.2)]",
    emerald: "border-emerald-500 shadow-[0_0_20px_rgba(16,185,129,0.2)]"
  };

  return (
    <div 
      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
      style={{ left: position.x, top: position.y }}
      className={`absolute w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-slate-950 border-2 ${borderColors[color]} flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-2 cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing z-10 select-none group transition-shadow hover:shadow-[0_0_30px_rgba(59,130,246,0.4)]`}
    >
      <Icon className="text-white" size={24} />
      <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white uppercase tracking-wide mt-1 bg-slate-900 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border border-slate-800">{label}</span>
      
      {/* Node Connection Points */}
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -right-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
      <div className="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-white border-2 border-slate-900 absolute -left-1.5 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2"></div>
    </div>
  );
};

const WorkflowView = () => {
  // Initial positions matching the screenshot curve roughly
  const [nodes, setNodes] = useState([
    { id: 1, label: "Start", icon: Zap, x: 100, y: 300, color: "emerald" },
    { id: 2, label: "Plan #1", icon: FileText, x: 300, y: 150, color: "blue" },
    { id: 3, label: "Video #2", icon: Video, x: 600, y: 150, color: "indigo" },
    { id: 4, label: "Publish #3", icon: Send, x: 800, y: 400, color: "cyan" }
  ]);

  const handleDrag = (id: number, newPos: {x: number, y: number}) => {
    setNodes(nodes.map(n => n.id === id ? { ...n, ...newPos } : n));
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-full bg-slate-950 relative overflow-hidden cursor-crosshair">
      {/* Background Grid */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(to_right,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px),linear-gradient(to_bottom,#1e293b_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:40px_40px] opacity-20 pointer-events-none" />

      <div className="absolute top-6 right-6 z-20 flex gap-3">
        <Button variant="secondary" icon={FileText}>Save Draft</Button>
        <Button icon={Plus}>Create Agent</Button>
      </div>

      {/* SVG Layer for Connections */}
      <svg className="absolute inset-0 w-full h-full pointer-events-none z-0">
        <defs>
          <linearGradient id="gradient" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
            <stop offset="0%" stopColor="#10b981" />
            <stop offset="50%" stopColor="#3b82f6" />
            <stop offset="100%" stopColor="#06b6d4" />
          </linearGradient>
        </defs>
        {nodes.map((node, i) => {
          if (i === nodes.length - 1) return null;
          const next = nodes[i+1];
          const startX = node.x + 96; // Right edge
          const startY = node.y + 48; // Center Y
          const endX = next.x;        // Left edge
          const endY = next.y + 48;   // Center Y
          
          const cp1X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;
          const cp2X = startX + (endX - startX) / 2;

          const d = `M ${startX} ${startY} C ${cp1X} ${startY}, ${cp2X} ${endY}, ${endX} ${endY}`;

          return (
            <g key={i}>
              {/* Glow Effect */}
              <path d={d} stroke="rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)" strokeWidth="8" fill="none" />
              {/* Main Line */}
              <path d={d} stroke="url(#gradient)" strokeWidth="3" fill="none" strokeLinecap="round" />
              {/* Animated Dash */}
              <path 
                d={d} 
                stroke="white" 
                strokeWidth="2" 
                fill="none" 
                strokeDasharray="4,8"
                className="opacity-50 animate-[dash_1s_linear_infinite]"
              />
            </g>
          )
        })}
      </svg>

      {/* Nodes */}
      {nodes.map(node => (
        <DraggableNode 
          key={node.id} 
          {...node} 
          onDrag={handleDrag} 
        />
      ))}

      {/* Zoom Controls */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-6 left-1/2 transform -translate-x-1/2 flex gap-1 p-1 bg-slate-900/90 border border-slate-800 rounded-lg backdrop-blur shadow-xl">
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomOut size={16} /></button>
        <span className="px-3 py-2 text-xs text-slate-300 font-mono flex items-center min-w-[50px] justify-center bg-slate-950 rounded">100%</span>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><ZoomIn size={16} /></button>
        <div className="w-px h-6 bg-slate-800 mx-1 self-center"></div>
        <button className="p-2 hover:bg-slate-800 rounded text-slate-400 transition-colors"><Maximize size={16} /></button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

      <Icon size={18} />
      {label}

};

Exploring bridgeMind.ai reveals it offers "Vibe Coding," an AI-assisted, natural-language programming approach for rapid prototyping, scaffolding, review, and deployment, focusing on flow-state coding. Next, I will summarize its main features.





I've explored the BridgeMind.ai website. Here's what I found:



Overview

BridgeMind is an educational platform focused on teaching "Vibe Coding" - a modern approach to software development that leverages AI-assisted programming and natural language to build applications.

What is Vibe Coding?

Vibe coding represents a paradigm shift in software development where developers describe features, user flows, and constraints in plain language, and AI tools (like ChatGPT, Claude, GitHub Copilot, and Cursor) generate the corresponding code. The approach emphasizes:

Flow-state coding with minimal context switching

Rapid prototyping - building functional prototypes in hours instead of weeks

Prompt engineering and human-in-the-loop code review

Quality and safety through validation, testing, and security best practices

Core Philosophy

The platform promotes moving from prompt → scaffold → review → ship quickly, allowing developers to build Next.js frontends, APIs, and tests while maintaining high standards for accessibility, performance, and security. It blends a calm, aesthetic coding experience with practical developer productivity.

Course Offerings

BridgeMind offers three structured learning tracks:

Vibe Coding Fundamentals (4 weeks) - Natural language to code, prompt patterns, review & tests, flow setup

Vibe Web Development (6 weeks) - Next.js with AI, UI prompts & components, Auth & APIs, deployment with CI

Prompt-to-Prototype (3 weeks) - Idea to outline to scaffold, iterate with critiques, ship MVP

Tools Covered

The platform teaches how to use various AI coding tools including ChatGPT, Claude, Claude Code, Cursor, GitHub Copilot, Replit, and VS Code extensions.

Sample Projects

Students learn to build practical applications like prompt-to-app starters, flow-state task managers, AI-powered chat interfaces, documentation RAG copilots, landing page generators, and AI review assistants.

Community

BridgeMind has an active community presence across YouTube, X (Twitter), Instagram, and TikTok, plus a Discord server for learners to connect and share experiences.

The platform positions itself as the bridge between traditional coding and the future of AI-assisted development, making software creation more accessible and efficient through natural language programming.
